This is a self-contained version of some solutions for HoTT-Book's exercises.
The idea is to unpackage all as long as possible to get a better understanding.
Many changes can appear running this experiment. Solutions are
type-checked as a whole using `Agda` `v2.5.3`.

## Requirements

`Agda` has a pragma to be compatible with HoTT:

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="551" class="Symbol">{-#</a> <a id="555" class="Keyword">OPTIONS</a> <a id="563" class="Option">--without-K</a> <a id="575" class="Symbol">#-}</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Equality type  also called Identity type can be defined as follows.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="673" class="Keyword">infix</a> <a id="679" class="Number">4</a> <a id="681" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#690" class="Datatype Operator">_≡_</a>
<a id="685" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="_≡_"></a><a id="690" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#690" class="Datatype Operator">_≡_</a> <a id="694" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="695" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#695" class="Bound">a</a><a id="696" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="698" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="699" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#699" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="701" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="703" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="707" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#695" class="Bound">a</a><a id="708" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="710" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="711" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#711" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="713" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="715" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#699" class="Bound">A</a><a id="716" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="718" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="720" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#699" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="722" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="724" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="728" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#695" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="730" class="Keyword">where</a>

## Chapter 1

### Exercise 1.1

{: .exercise }
  Given functions $f : A \rightarrow B$ and $g : B \to C$, define
  their composite $g\circ f:A\to C$.
  Show that we have $h \circ (g\circ f) \equiv (h\circ g)\circ f$.

We define the composition operation in `Agda` as follows.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="_∘_"></a><a id="2008" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2008" class="Function Operator">_∘_</a> <a id="2012" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2014" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="2016" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2017" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2017" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="2019" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2019" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="2021" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2021" class="Bound">k</a><a id="2022" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="2024" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2025" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2025" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="2027" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2029" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="2033" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2017" class="Bound">i</a><a id="2034" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="2036" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2036" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="2038" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2040" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="2044" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2019" class="Bound">j</a><a id="2045" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="2047" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2047" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="2049" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2051" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="2055" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2021" class="Bound">k</a><a id="2056" class="Symbol">}</a>

### Exercise 1.2

{: .exercise }
  Derive the recursion principle for products $\rec_{A\times B}$
  using only the projections, and verify that the definitional equalities
  are valid. Do the same for $\Sigma$-types.

To solve this problem we need to know:

  - The recursion principle for Σ-types:

    {:.eq}
      $$ \rec_{ A \times B}
        : \prod\limits_{C : \U} (A \to B \to C) → A \times B \to C.
      $$

  - The recursion principle for Σ-types:

    <p class="equation">
    $ \rec_{\sum\limits_{(x : A) } B(x)}
      : \prod\limits_{(C : U)} (\Pi_{(x : A)} B(x) \rightarrow C) \rightarrow
        \sum_{(x : A)} B(x) \rightarrow C
    $
    </p>

<div class="proof" id="proof-1.2">
Proof.<br/>
For products:<br/>
If we have the projections,
$\proj_1 : A \times B \to \mathsf{A}$ and $\proj_2 : A \times B \to \mathsf{B}$,
then $\rec_2$ is another inhabitant where

<p class="equation">
$
\begin{align*}
&\rec_1 : \prod\limits_{C : \U} (A \to B \to C) \to A \times B \to C\\
&\rec_1~C~g~c~:\equiv~g~(\proj_1 c,~\proj_2 c).
\end{align*}
$
</p>
By reflexivity, we prove the equality between $\rec_{ A \times B}$ and $\rec_1$.
<br/>
<br/>
For sums:<br/>
The projections are $\proj_1 : \sum_{x : A}  Bx \to \mathsf{A}$ and
$\proj_2 :  \prod {(p : \sum_{x : A}  Bx)} \to \mathsf{B} (\proj_1 p)$.<br/>
By using these projections, we got another recursor defined as follows:
<p class="equation">
$$
\begin{align*}
&\rec_2 : \prod\limits_{C : \U}  (\prod_{x : A} Bx \to C) \to \sum\limits_{x : A} B x \to C\\
&\rec_2~C~g~c~=~g~(\proj_1 c)~(\proj_2 c)
\end{align*}
$$
</p>

By reflexivity, we prove the equality between $\rec_{\sum\limits_{(x : A) } B(x)}$ and $\rec_2$.
</div>

Now, I'm gonna use the universe levels from Agda in
the following exercises, including this one:

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="4195" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="4200" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="4207" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Primitive.html" class="Module">Agda.Primitive</a>
  <a id="4224" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="4230" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4231" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Primitive.html#408" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="4236" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="4238" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Primitive.html#657" class="Primitive Operator">_⊔_</a><a id="4241" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="4243" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Primitive.html#611" class="Primitive">lzero</a><a id="4248" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="4250" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Primitive.html#627" class="Primitive">lsuc</a><a id="4254" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Σ-type (sigma type) definition (see the definition without projections
[here](https://github.com/jonaprieto/hott-book/blob/master/other/prelim.agda#L20)):

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="4437" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Σ-Def₁"></a><a id="4444" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4444" class="Module">Σ-Def₁</a> <a id="4451" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="4460" class="Keyword">record</a> <a id="Σ-Def₁.Σ"></a><a id="4467" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4467" class="Record">Σ</a> <a     <a id="4527" class="Keyword">constructor</a> <a id="Σ-Def₁.Σ._,_"></a><a id="4539" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4539" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a>
    <a id="4547" class="Keyword">field</a>
      <a id="Σ-Def₁.Σ.proj₁"></a><a id="4559" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4559" class="Field">proj₁</a> <a id="4565" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4567" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4476" class="Bound">A</a>
      <a id="Σ-Def₁.Σ.proj₂"></a><a id="4575" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4575" class="Field">proj₂</a> <a id="4581" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4583" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4488" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="4585" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4559" class="Field">proj₁</a>

  <a id="4594" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="4599" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4467" class="Module">Σ</a> <a id="4601" class="Keyword">public</a>
<a id="4608" class="Comment">-- _,_ : (proj₁ : A) → B proj₁ → Σ A B.</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Its recursor with a function $g : \prod_{(x : A)} B(x)\rightarrow C$
that we provide.

On the other hand, the product type is just a particular case of the sigma type
when the codomain is not dependent, as we can see next by omitting the argument
in `(λ _ → B)`.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="5231" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="×-Def₁"></a><a id="5238" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#5238" class="Module">×-Def₁</a> <a id="5245" class="Keyword">where</a>

### Exercise 1.3

<p class="exercise">
Derive the induction principle for products $\mathsf{ind}_{A\times B}$,
using only the projections and the propositional uniqueness principle
$\mathsf{uniq}_{A\times B}$.
Verify that the definitional equalities are valid.
</p>

To solve this problem, recall the uniqueness principle (Pp. 29. HoTT-Book)

- The **propositional uniqueness principle** says that
every element of $A\times B$ is equal to a pair.

<p class="equation">
  $ \mathsf{uniq}_{A\times B}
     : \prod_{(x : A \times B)} ((\proj_{1}(x) , \proj_{2}(x))
       \equiv_{A\times B} x).
  $
</p>

Product type definition using `data`:

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="6374" class="Comment">-- this would be trivial in agda due to definitional η for records</a>
<a id="6441" class="Comment">-- so Capriotti defined a product type without η:</a>

Projections and $\mathsf{uniq}_{A\times B}$:

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="6828" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="×-Fun₂"></a><a id="6835" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#6835" class="Module">×-Fun₂</a> <a id="6842" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6843" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#6843" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="6845" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#6845" class="Bound">j</a><a id="6846" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="6848" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#6848" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="6850" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6852" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="6856" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#6843" class="Bound">i</a><a id="6857" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="6859" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#6859" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="6861" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6863" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="6867" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#6845" class="Bound">j</a><a id="6868" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6870" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="6878" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="6883" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#6498" class="Module">×-Def₂</a> <a id="6890" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="6896" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="6898" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#6519" class="Datatype Operator">_×_</a><a id="6901" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="6902" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#6575" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a><a id="6905" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="6907" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#6598" class="Function">proj₁</a><a id="6912" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="6914" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#6679" class="Function">proj₂</a><a id="6919" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="6924" class="Comment">-- propositional uniqueness principle:</a>

  <a id="7373" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7285" class="Function">pair=</a> <a id="7379" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#738" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="7384" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#738" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="7389" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7391" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#738" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

The induction principle for the product type:

<p class="equation">
$\mathsf{ind}_{A\times B} : \prod\limits_{C : A \times B \to \U}
  \left( \prod\limits_{x:A}\ \prod\limits_{y:B}\ \,C( (x,y) ) \right)
  \to \prod\limits_{x:A \times B}\ \,C(x)
$
</p>

        <a id="7834" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7836" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="7838" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7838" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7840" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7842" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7694" class="Bound">A</a><a id="7843" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="7845" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7845" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="7847" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7849" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7705" class="Bound">B</a><a id="7850" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7852" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7854" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7807" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="7856" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7857" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7838" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7859" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#6575" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="7861" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7845" class="Bound">y</a><a id="7862" class="Symbol">))</a>

<p class="exercise">
Generalize $\mathsf{uniq}_{A\times B}$ to Σ-types, and do the same for
$\Sigma$-types, i.e. show induction and verify that the definitional equality
is valid.
</p>

Σ-type definition using `data`:

Projections and uniqueness propositional principle:

  <a id="8608" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="8613" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#8367" class="Module">Σ-Def₂</a> <a id="8620" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="8626" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8627" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#8388" class="Datatype">Σ</a><a id="8628" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="8630" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#8446" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a> <a id="8634" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="9233" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#9082" class="Function">ind-β</a> <a id="9239" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#9239" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="9241" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#9241" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="9243" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#9243" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="9245" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#9245" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="9247" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9249" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#738" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

### Exercise 1.4

<div class="exercise">
Assuming as given only the <em>iterator</em> for natural numbers
<p class="equation">
$\mathsf{ite} : \prod\limits_{C:\U} C \to (C \to C) \to \N \to C $
</p>
with the defining equations
<p class="equation">
$
\begin{align*}
\mathsf{ite}(C,c_0,c_s,0)               &\equiv c_0, \\
\mathsf{ite}(C,c_0,c_s,\mathsf{suc}(n)) &\equiv c_s(\mathsf{ite}(C,c_0,c_s,n)),
\end{align*}
$
</p>
derive a function having the type of the recursor $\rec$.
Show that the defining equations of the recursor hold propositionally for this
function, using the induction principle for $\N$.
</div>

To solve this problem, let us define the recursor and also the induction principle
for natural numbers. (See more details about these functions in
[Induction on Natural Numbers]({% post_url 2018-02-12-induction-on-natural-numbers %})).

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="10132" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="ℕ-Def"></a><a id="10139" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10139" class="Module">ℕ-Def</a> <a id="10145" class="Keyword">where</a>

Now, we define the iterator following the equations above:

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="10652" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="ℕ-Fun"></a><a id="10659" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10659" class="Module">ℕ-Fun</a> <a id="10665" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="10673" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="10678" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10139" class="Module">ℕ-Def</a> <a id="10684" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="10690" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10691" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10159" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="10692" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="10694" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10177" class="InductiveConstructor">zero</a><a id="10698" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="10700" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10190" class="InductiveConstructor">suc</a><a id="10703" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="10707" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="10712" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10211" class="Module">ℕ-Rec</a> <a id="10718" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="10724" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10725" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10238" class="Function">rec</a><a id="10728" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="ℕ-Fun.ite"></a><a id="10733" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10733" class="Function">ite</a> <a id="10737" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10739" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="10741" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10742" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10742" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="10744" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10746" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="10749" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10751" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10753" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10742" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="10755" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10757" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10758" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10742" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="10760" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10762" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10742" class="Bound">C</a><a id="10763" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10765" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10767" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10159" class="Datatype">ℕ</a> <a id="10769" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10771" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10742" class="Bound">C</a>
  <a id="10775" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10733" class="Function">ite</a> <a id="10779" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10779" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="10781" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10781" class="Bound">c₀</a> <a id="10784" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10784" class="Bound">cₛ</a> <a id="10787" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10177" class="InductiveConstructor">zero</a>    <a id="10795" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10797" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10781" class="Bound">c₀</a>
  <a id="10802" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10733" class="Function">ite</a> <a id="10806" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10806" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="10808" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10808" class="Bound">c₀</a> <a id="10811" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10811" class="Bound">cₛ</a> <a id="10814" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10815" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10190" class="InductiveConstructor">suc</a> <a id="10819" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10819" class="Bound">n</a><a id="10820" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10822" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10824" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10811" class="Bound">cₛ</a> <a id="10827" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10828" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10733" class="Function">ite</a> <a id="10832" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10806" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="10834" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10808" class="Bound">c₀</a> <a id="10837" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10811" class="Bound">cₛ</a> <a id="10840" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10819" class="Bound">n</a><a id="10841" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Then, we now can define the recursor using this `ite` by iterating over the type
`ℕ × C` (*reloading recursion*?).


<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="10985" class="Comment">-- recursor</a>

           <a id="11238" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11111" class="Bound">n</a><a id="11239" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Now, we need to establish the propositional equality between these two
definitions of recursor, i.e, between `rec` and `rec₂`. Let's use
induction to prove that.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="11429" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="ex1-4"></a><a id="11436" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11436" class="Module">ex1-4</a> <a id="11442" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="11451" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="11456" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10139" class="Module">ℕ-Def</a> <a id="11462" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="11468" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11469" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10159" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="11470" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="11472" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10177" class="InductiveConstructor">zero</a><a id="11476" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="11478" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10190" class="InductiveConstructor">suc</a><a id="11481" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="11485" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="11490" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10211" class="Module">ℕ-Rec</a> <a id="11496" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="11502" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11503" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10238" class="Function">rec</a><a id="11506" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="11510" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="11515" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10362" class="Module">ℕ-Ind</a> <a id="11521" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="11527" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11528" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10389" class="Function">ind</a><a id="11531" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="11535" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="11540" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10659" class="Module">ℕ-Fun</a> <a id="11546" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="11552" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11553" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10733" class="Function">ite</a><a id="11556" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="11558" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11045" class="Function">rec₂</a><a id="11562" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="11567" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="11572" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#6498" class="Module">×-Def₂</a> <a id="11579" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="11585" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11586" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#6519" class="Datatype Operator">_×_</a><a id="11589" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="11591" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#6598" class="Function">proj₁</a><a id="11596" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="11598" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#6679" class="Function">proj₂</a><a id="11603" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="11605" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#6575" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a><a id="11608" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="ex1-4.proof"></a><a id="11627" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11627" class="Function">proof</a> <a id="11633" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11635" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11636" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11636" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="11638" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11640" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="11643" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="11645" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11645" class="Bound">c₀</a> <a id="11648" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11650" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11636" class="Bound">C</a><a id="11651" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="11653" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11653" class="Bound">cₛ</a> <a id="11656" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11658" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10159" class="Datatype">ℕ</a> <a id="11660" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11662" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11636" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="11664" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11666" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11636" class="Bound">C</a><a id="11667" class="Symbol">)</a>
        <a id="11677" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11679" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="11681" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11682" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link ### Exercise 1.5

{: .exercise}

  Show that if we define $$A+B :\equiv \sum\limits_{(x : \two)} \rec_{\two} (\U, A , B, x),$$
  then we can give a definition of $\ind_{A + B}$ for which the
  definitional equalities holds.

To solve this problem, let me introduce the $\two$ type, which is, the
type only two constructors, the **Booleans**.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="12545" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="𝟚-Def₁"></a><a id="12552" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12552" class="Module">𝟚-Def₁</a> <a id="12559" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="12568" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="𝟚-Def₁.𝟚"></a><a id="12573" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12573" class="Datatype">𝟚</a> <a id="12575" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12577" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="12581" class="Keyword">where</a>
    <a id="𝟚-Def₁.𝟚.𝟘"></a><a id="12591" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12591" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟘</a> <a id="12593" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12595" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12573" class="Datatype">𝟚</a>
    <a id="𝟚-Def₁.𝟚.𝟙"></a><a id="12601" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12601" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟙</a> <a id="12603" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12605" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12573" class="Datatype">𝟚</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


With the recursor:

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="12653" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="𝟚-Rec₁"></a><a id="12660" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12660" class="Module">𝟚-Rec₁</a> <a id="12667" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="13457" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13418" class="Function">inr</a> <a id="13461" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13461" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="13463" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13465" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13466" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12601" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟙</a> <a id="13468" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4539" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="13470" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13461" class="Bound">b</a><a id="13471" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


Now, let's try to define the recursor for this coproduct, and later,
we'll try the dependent version of it to complete the exercise.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="13633" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="+-Rec₁"></a><a id="13640" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13640" class="Module">+-Rec₁</a> <a id="13647" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="13656" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="13661" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13105" class="Module">+-Def₁</a> <a id="13668" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="13674" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13675" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13225" class="Function Operator">_+_</a><a id="13678" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="13680" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13360" class="Function">inl</a><a id="13683" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="13684" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13418" class="Function">inr</a><a id="13687" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="13688" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4539" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a><a id="13691" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="13695" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="13700" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12552" class="Module">𝟚-Def₁</a> <a id="13707" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="13713" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13714" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12591" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟘</a><a id="13715" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="13716" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12601" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟙</a><a id="13717" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="13718" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12573" class="Datatype">𝟚</a><a id="13719" class="Symbol">)</a>

      <a id="13770" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13772" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13773" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13739" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="13775" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13777" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13753" class="Bound">C</a><a id="13778" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="13786" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13788" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13789" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13741" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="13791" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13793" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13753" class="Bound">C</a><a id="13794" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="13802" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13804" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13739" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="13806" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13225" class="Function Operator">+</a> <a id="13808" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13741" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="13810" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13812" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13753" class="Bound">C</a>
  <a id="13816" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13724" class="Function">rec</a> <a id="13820" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13820" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="13822" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13822" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="13824" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13825" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12591" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟘</a> <a id="13827" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4539" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="13829" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13829" class="Bound">a</a><a id="13830" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13832" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13834" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13820" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="13836" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13829" class="Bound">a</a>
  <a id="13840" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13724" class="Function">rec</a> <a id="13844" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13844" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="13846" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13846" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="13848" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13849" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12601" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟙</a> <a id="13851" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4539" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="13853" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13853" class="Bound">b</a><a id="13854" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13856" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13858" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13846" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="13860" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13853" class="Bound">b</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Notice how the recursor of the coproduct matches with the elimination
rule of the disjunction conective also called *case analysis*. That's follows from the
[**propositions-as-types**](https://ncatlab.org/nlab/show/propositions+as+types).

![path](/assets/latexit-images/disj-elimination.png){: width="%50" }

Finally, the induction principle for the coproduct:

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="14250" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="+-Ind₁"></a><a id="14257" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14257" class="Module">+-Ind₁</a> <a id="14264" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="14273" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="14278" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13105" class="Module">+-Def₁</a> <a id="14285" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="14291" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14292" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13225" class="Function Operator">_+_</a><a id="14295" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="14297" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13360" class="Function">inl</a><a id="14300" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="14301" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13418" class="Function">inr</a><a id="14304" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="14306" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4539" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a><a id="14309" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="14313" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="14318" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12552" class="Module">𝟚-Def₁</a> <a id="14325" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="14331" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14332" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12591" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟘</a><a id="14333" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="14334" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12601" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟙</a><a id="14335" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="14336" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12573" class="Datatype">𝟚</a><a id="14337" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="+-Ind₁.ind"></a><a id="14342" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14342" class="Function">ind</a> <a id="14346" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14348" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="14350" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14351" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14351" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="14353" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14353" class="Bound">j</a><a id="14354" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14356" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14357" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14357" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="14359" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14359" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="14361" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14363" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="14367" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14351" class="Bound">i</a><a id="14368" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14370" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14371" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14371" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="14373" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14375" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14357" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="14377" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13225" class="Function Operator">+</a> <a id="14379" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14359" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="14381" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14383" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="14387" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14353" class="Bound">j</a><a id="14388" class="Symbol">}</a>
      <a id="14396" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14398" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="14400" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14400" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="14402" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14404" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14357" class="Bound">A</a><a id="14405" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14407" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14409" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14371" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="14411" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14412" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13360" class="Function">inl</a> <a id="14416" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14400" class="Bound">a</a><a id="14417" class="Symbol">))</a>
      <a id="14426" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14428" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="14430" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14430" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="14432" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14434" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14359" class="Bound">B</a><a id="14435" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14437" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14439" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14371" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="14441" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14442" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13418" class="Function">inr</a> <a id="14446" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14430" class="Bound">b</a><a id="14447" class="Symbol">))</a>

### Exercise 1.6

<div class="exercise" id="ex-1.6">
Show that if we define $A \times B :≡ \prod_{x:\mathbf{2}}\rec_{\mathbf{2}}\ (\U\, A\, B\, x)$,
then we can give a definition of $\mathsf{ind}_{A\times B}$ for which the definitional
equalities propositionally (i.e. using equality types).
</div>

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="15233" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="×-Def₃"></a><a id="15240" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#15240" class="Module">×-Def₃</a> <a id="15247" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="15255" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="15260" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12552" class="Module">𝟚-Def₁</a> <a id="15267" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="15273" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15274" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12591" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟘</a><a id="15275" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="15276" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12601" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟙</a><a id="15277" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="15278" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12573" class="Datatype">𝟚</a><a id="15279" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15281" class="Keyword">public</a>

### Exercise 1.8

<div class="exercise" id="exercise-1.8">

Define multiplication and exponentiation using $\rec{\N}$.
Verify that $(\N,+,0,\times,1)$ is a semiring using only
$\ind{\N}$.

</div>


<div class="proof" markdown="1">
Solution.<br/>
Operation definitions:

}}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#17326" class="Bound">m</a> <a id="17328" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17330" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10159" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="17331" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17333" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="17335" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10159" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="17336" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17338" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="17341" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#17341" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="17343" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="17345" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10190" class="InductiveConstructor">suc</a> <a id="17349" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10177" class="InductiveConstructor">zero</a><a id="17353" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17355" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="17358" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#17358" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="17360" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#17360" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="17362" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#17362" class="Bound">m</a> <a id="17364" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="17366" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#17201" class="Function">multi</a> <a id="17372" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#17362" class="Bound">m</a> <a id="17374" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17375" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#17360" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="17377" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#17362" class="Bound">m</a><a id="17378" class="Symbol">))</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

On the other hand, a **semiring** is a type? together with two binary operators S(+,*) satisfying the following conditions:

1. Additive associativity: $\prod_{a,b,c : S} (a+b)+c=a+(b+c)$.

2. Additive commutativity: $\prod_{a,b : S}  a+b=b+a$.

3. Multiplicative associativity: $$\prod_{a,b,c : S} (a*b)*c=a*(b*c)$$.

4. Left and right distributivity:

$$\prod_{a,b,c : S} a*(b+c)=(a*b)+(a*c)\text{  and  } \prod_{a,b,c : S} (b+c)*a=(b*a)+(c*a).$$

</div>

### Exercise 1.9

<div class="exercise" id="exercise-1.9">

Define the type family $\mathsf{Fin} : \N \to \U$ mentioned
at the end of Section 1.3, and the dependent function $\mathsf{fmax} :
\prod_{n:\N} \mathsf{Fin}(n+1)$ mentioned in Section 1.4.
</div>

### Exercise 1.11

<div class="exercise" id="exercise-1.11">
Show that for any type $A$, we have $\neg\neg\neg A \to \neg A$.
</div>

A propositional logic proof using [Agda-Prop](http://github.com/jonaprieto/agda-prop)
library:

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="19270" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Ex1-11"></a><a id="19277" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19277" class="Module">Ex1-11</a> <a id="19284" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="19292" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="19297" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="19304" href="Data.PropFormula.html" class="Module">Data.PropFormula</a> <a id="19321" class="Number">1</a>

  <a id="Ex1-11.proof"></a><a id="19326" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19326" class="Function">proof</a> <a id="19332" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19334" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="19336" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19337" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19337" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="19338" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19340" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19341" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19341" class="Bound">A</a><a id="19342" class="Symbol">}</a>
        <a id="19352" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19354" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19337" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="19356" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#1657" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="19358" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="19360" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="19362" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="19364" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19341" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="19366" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#919" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⊃</a> <a id="19368" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="19370" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19341" class="Bound">A</a>
  <a id="19374" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19326" class="Function">proof</a> <a id="19380" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19381" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19381" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="19382" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19384" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19384" class="Bound">A</a><a id="19385" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19387" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="19393" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#3276" class="InductiveConstructor">⊃-intro</a>
      <a id="19407" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19408" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#2276" class="InductiveConstructor">¬-intro</a>
          <a id="19426" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19427" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#2387" class="InductiveConstructor">¬-elim</a>
              <a id="19448" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19449" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#1868" class="InductiveConstructor">weaken</a> <a id="19456" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19384" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="19458" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19459" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#1706" class="InductiveConstructor">assume</a> <a id="19466" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19467" class="Argument">Γ</a> <a id="19469" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19471" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19381" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="19472" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19474" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19475" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="19477" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19478" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="19480" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19481" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="19483" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19384" class="Bound">A</a><a id="19484" class="Symbol">)))))</a>
              <a id="19504" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19505" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#2276" class="InductiveConstructor">¬-intro</a>
                <a id="19529" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19530" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#2387" class="InductiveConstructor">¬-elim</a>
                  <a id="19555" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19556" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#1706" class="InductiveConstructor">assume</a> <a id="19563" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19564" class="Argument">Γ</a> <a id="19566" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19568" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19381" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="19570" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#1170" class="Function Operator">,</a> <a id="19572" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="19574" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="19576" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="19578" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19384" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="19580" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#1170" class="Function Operator">,</a> <a id="19582" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19384" class="Bound">A</a><a id="19583" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19585" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19586" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="19588" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19384" class="Bound">A</a><a id="19589" class="Symbol">))</a>
                  <a id="19610" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19611" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#1868" class="InductiveConstructor">weaken</a> <a id="19618" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19619" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="19621" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19384" class="Bound">A</a><a id="19622" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19624" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19625" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#1706" class="InductiveConstructor">assume</a> <a id="19632" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19633" class="Argument">Γ</a> <a id="19635" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19637" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19381" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="19639" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#1170" class="Function Operator">,</a> <a id="19641" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="19643" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="19645" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="19647" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19384" class="Bound">A</a><a id="19648" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19650" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19384" class="Bound">A</a><a id="19651" class="Symbol">))))))</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

In type theory, the term is:

$$
λ (x : ((A → ⊥) → ⊥) → ⊥) (a : A) . x ((λ h : A → ⊥) . ha) :
((A → ⊥) → ⊥) → ⊥) → (A → ⊥)
$$

### Exercise 1.16

<div class="exercise" id="exercise-1.16">
Show that addition of natural numbers is commutative:
$\prod\limits_{i,j : \N}\ (i + j = j + i).$
</div>

Hint: by induction twice.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="20004" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Ex1-16"></a><a id="20011" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20011" class="Module">Ex1-16</a> <a id="20018" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="20026" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="20031" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10139" class="Module">ℕ-Def</a>
  <a id="20039" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="20044" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10362" class="Module">ℕ-Ind</a>
  <a id="20052" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="20057" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#17095" class="Module">Ex1-8</a> <a id="20063" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="20069" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20070" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#17136" class="Function Operator">_+_</a><a id="20073" class="Symbol">)</a>

                      <a id="20821" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20636" class="Bound">hyp₂</a><a id="20825" class="Symbol">)))</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## Chapter 2

### Exercise 2.6

<div class="exercise" id="exercise-2.6">
Prove that if $p : x \equiv y$, then the function
$(p \cdot -) : (y \equiv z) \to (x \equiv z)$ is an equivalence.
</div>

![path-triangle](/assets/ipe-images/path-triangle.png){: width="%30" }

<div class="proof">
Solution. <br/>

To show the equivalence, it suffices to show a function
$g : x \equiv z \to y \equiv z$ such that we can prove
$ (p \cdot -) \circ g \sim \id_{x \equiv z}$ and
$ g \circ (p \cdot -) \sim \id_{y \equiv z}$.

Let's define the function $g$.
<p class="equation">
$
\begin{align*}
&g : x ≡ z → y ≡ z\\
&g~m~=~\trans~(\sym~p)~m
\end{align*}
$
</p>
<br/>

($(p \cdot -) \circ g \sim \id_{x \equiv z}$):
Let be $m : x ≡ z$, we have,

<p class="equation">
$
\begin{align*}
(p \cdot -) \circ g (m) &= (p \cdot -)~(g~m)\\
                        &= (p \cdot -)~(\trans~(\sym~p)~m)\\
                        &= \trans~p~(\trans~(\sym~p)~m)\\
                        &= \trans~(\trans~p~(\sym~p))~m\\
                        &= \trans~\refl_{x≡z}~m\\
                        &= m
\end{align*}
$
</p>
<br/>
($ g \circ (p \cdot -) \sim \id_{y \equiv z}$):
Let be $n : y ≡ z$, we have,

<p class="equation">
$
\begin{align*}
g \circ (p \cdot -) n &= g (\trans~p~n)\\
                      &= (\trans~(\sym~p)~(\trans~p~n)\\
                      &= \trans~(\trans~(\sym~p)~p)~n\\
                      &= \trans~\refl_{y ≡ z}~n\\
                      &= n.
\end{align*}
$
</p>

</div>


### Exercise 2.10

<div class="exercise" id="exercise-2.10">
Prove that ∑-types are associative, in that for any $A : \U$
and families $B : A  \to U$ and $C : \sum_{(x : A)} B(x) \to \U$,
we have
<p class="equation">
$\sum\limits_{(x : A)} \sum\limits_{(y : B(x))} C((x,y)) \simeq \sum\limits_{p : \sum_{x:A} B(x)} C(p)$.
</p>
</div>

<div class="proof" id="proof-2.10">
Solution.<br/>
We can prove that the following functions $f$ and $g$ are inverses.

<p class="equation">
$\sum\limits_{(x : A)} \sum\limits_{(y : B(x))} C((x,y)) \overset{f}{\underset{g}{\rightleftarrows}} \sum\limits_{p : \sum_{x:A} B(x)} C(p)$.
</p>
defined by $f(a,b,c) :\equiv ((a,b),c)$ and $g(z,c) :\equiv (\proj_1 z,\proj_{2} z, c)$.<br/>
Indeed,
<p class="equation">
$
\begin{align*}
(f \circ g) (z, c) &:\equiv f (g (z,c))\\
&:\equiv f\,(\proj_1 z,\proj_{2} z, c)\\
&:\equiv ((\proj_1 z,\proj_{2} z), c)
\end{align*}
$
</p>
</div>

  <a id="Σ-Fun₁.f-g"></a><a id="23609" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23609" class="Function">f-g</a> <a id="23613" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23615" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="23617" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23618" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23618" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="23620" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23622" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="23625" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="23627" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23628" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23628" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="23630" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23632" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23618" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="23634" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23636" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="23639" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="23641" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23642" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23642" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="23644" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23646" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4467" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="23648" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23618" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="23650" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23628" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="23652" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23654" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="23657" class="Symbol">}</a>
        <a id="23667" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23669" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23670" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23670" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="23672" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23674" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4467" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="23676" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23677" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4467" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="23679" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23618" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="23681" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23628" class="Bound">B</a><a id="23682" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="23684" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23642" class="Bound">C</a><a id="23685" class="Symbol">)</a>
        <a id="23695" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23697" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23308" class="Function">f</a> <a id="23699" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23700" class="Argument">A</a> <a id="23702" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="23704" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23618" class="Bound">A</a><a id="23705" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="23707" class="Argument">B</a> <a id="23709" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="23711" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23628" class="Bound">B</a><a id="23712" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="23714" class="Argument">C</a> <a id="23716" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="23718" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23642" class="Bound">C</a><a id="23719" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="23721" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23722" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23449" class="Function">g</a> <a id="23724" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23670" class="Bound">x</a><a id="23725" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="23727" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#690" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="23729" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23670" class="Bound">x</a>
  <a id="23733" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23609" class="Function">f-g</a> <a id="23737" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23737" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="23739" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="23741" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#738" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>

  <a id="Σ-Fun₁.g-f"></a><a id="23749" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23749" class="Function">g-f</a> <a id="23753" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23755" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="23757" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23758" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23758" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="23760" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23762" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="23765" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="23767" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23768" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23768" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="23770" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23772" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23758" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="23774" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23776" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="23779" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="23781" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23782" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23782" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="23784" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23786" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4467" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="23788" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23758" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="23790" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23768" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="23792" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23794" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="23797" class="Symbol">}</a>
        <a id="23807" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23809" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23810" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23810" ### Exercise 2.13

<div class="exercise" id="exercise-2.13">
Show that $(\two \simeq \two) \simeq \two$.
</div>

<div class="proof" markdown="1">
Solution.<br/>

The following text is from [Jdoughertyii](https://github.com/jdoughertyii/hott-exercises/blob/master/Ch02.v).<br/>
The result essentially says that $\two$ is equivalent to itself in two ways:
the identity provides one equivalence, and negation gives the other.  So we
first define these.  $\id_{\two}$ is its own quasi-inverse; we have
$\id_{\two} \circ \id_{\two} \equiv \id_{\two}$, so $\id_{\two}
\circ \id_{\two}
\sim \id_{\two}$ easily.  $\lnot$ is also its own quasi-inverse, since for
any $x$, $\lnot\lnot x = x$.
To show the result, we need to map $\id_{\two}$ and $\lnot$ onto $\two$ is
a quasi-invertible way.  But we need to define this map on all of $\two \simeq \two$.
So for any $h : \two\simeq \two$, let $f(h) = h(\zero_{\two})$, and define
$g : \two \to (\two \simeq \two)$ by

{: .equation}
  $$ g(\zero_{\two}) = \id_{\two}$$ and  $$g(\one_{\two}) = \lnot.$$

To show that these are quasi-inverses,
note first that whatever else is the case, an equivalence
$\two \simeq \two$ can't be a constant function, which we can prove by a case
analysis. Each of $f(\zero_{\two})$ and $f(\one_{\two})$ is in $\two$, so it is
either $\zero_{\two}$ or $\one_{\two}$.

So we have the cases:
 - $f(\zero_{\two}) = f(\one_{\two})$, in which case we can apply $f^{-1}$ to either side to get a contradiction, or
 - $f(\zero_{\two}) = \lnot f(\one_{\two})$. In which case we have the result
Showing that $f \circ g \sim \id_{\two}$ is easy, since we can do it by
cases.  We have

$$\begin{align*}
  f(g(\zero_{\two})) &= f(\id_{\two}) = \id_{\two}(\zero_{\two}) = \zero_{\two}
  \\
  f(g(\one_{\two})) &= f(\lnot) = \lnot \zero_{\two} = \one_{\two}
\end{align*}$$

For the other direction, suppose that $h : \two \simeq \two$ and that
function extensionality holds.
$h(\zero_{\two})$ is either $\zero_{\two}$ or $\one_{\two}$.  If the first, then
because $h$ isn't constant we have $h(\one_{\two}) = \lnot h(\zero_{\two}) =
\one_{\two}$, hence $h = \id_{\two}$.  Furthermore,

$$g(f(h)) = g(h(\zero_{\two})) = g(\zero_{\two}) = \id_\two = h$$

The same argument works for the other case. So $f$ is an equivalence, and
$(\two \simeq \two) \simeq \two$.

</div>

### Exercise 2.14

{: .exercise}

  Suppose we add to type theory [the equality reflection
  rule](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=IlfQjWqrK6I) which says that if there is
  an element $p : \id(x,y) $, then in fact $ x :\equiv y$. Prove that
  for any $p : \id(x,x)$ we have $p \equiv \refl_x$.

  ![path](/assets/latexit-images/hott-ex2.14.png){: width="25%" }


{: .proof}
  Proof.<br/>
  We first fix the type of $$\refl_x$$ in order to apply effectively
  path induction.<br/>
  ![path](/assets/latexit-images/hott-ex2.14b.png){: width="100%" }
  Now, $$\refl_x$$ and $$p : x = y$$ in the formulation of path induction
  are well-typed. Therefore, by path induction, we show that
  $$\id(p,\mathsf{refl_{x}})$$. Let be $$x : A$$ and $$C :\equiv
  \prod_{y : A} \prod_{p : x \equiv y }\ p \equiv \refl_{x}$$.
  It sufficies to show and inhabitant of $$C(x, \refl_{x})$$, and this is
  $$\refl_{\refl_x} : \refl_x = \refl_x$$.
  By the equation reflection rule, since we have an inhabitant of $$p \equiv
  \refl_x$$, we conclude these terms are judgemental equal, i.e., $$p \equiv \refl_x$$.

### Exercise 2.17

<div class="exercise">
<ul>
  <li> Show that if $A \simeq A$  and $B \simeq B'$, then $(A\times B) \simeq (A'\times B')$. </li>
  <li> Give two proofs of this fact, one using univalence and one not using it, and show that the two proofs are equal.</li>
  <li> Formulate and prove analogous results for the other type formers: $\Sigma$, $\to$, $\Pi$, and $+$. </li>
</ul>
</div>

<div class="proof" markdown="1">
  Proof.<br/>
  - Assuming Univalence.
  ![path](/assets/latexit-images/hott-ex2.17.png){: width="50%" }
  - Without Univalence, it is easy to prove
  that the function $h$ defined as follows gives us the
  equivalence that we are looking for.
  $$\begin{align*}
  &h : (A\times B) \to (A'\times B')\\
  &h (a , b) = (f\, a, g\, b).
  \end{align*}$$
  With the inverse:
  $$\begin{align*}
  &h^{-1} : (A'\times B') \to (A\times B)\\
  &h^{-1} (a , b) = (f^{-1}\, a, g^{-1}\, b).
  \end{align*}$$
  To prove these proofs are equal it is suffices to
  show these underlying functions are equal.
</div>

## Chapter 3

To solve the following exercises, let us recall a few things:

- The *set* definition in HoTT:

A type $A$ is a **set** if for all $x, y : A$ and
all $p, q : x \equiv y$, we have $ p \equiv q$. In a proposition
we have

$$\mathsf{isSet}(A) :\equiv \prod\limits_{(x,y : A)}\prod\limits_{(p,q : x \equiv y)} (p \equiv q).$$

- The type for equivalence from $A$ to $B$

$$ (A \simeq B) :\equiv \sum\limits_{f : A \to B} \mathsf{isequiv}(f), $$
where
$$
\mathsf{isequiv(f)} :\equiv
  \left (\sum\limits_{g : B \to A} (f \circ g \sim \id_{B})\right) \times
  \left (\sum\limits_{h : B \to A} (h \circ f \sim \id_{A})\right)
$$

- The homotopy concept:

Let $f , g : \prod\limits_{(x:A)} P(x)$ be two sections of a
type family $P : A \to \U$. A **homotopy** from $f$ to $g$
is a dependent function of type

$$(f \sim g) :\equiv \prod\limits_{x : A} (f(x) \equiv g(x)).$$

### Exercise 3.1

{: .exercise"}
  Prove that if $A\simeq B$ and $A$ is a set, then so is $B$.


<div class="proof" id="proof-3.1" markdown="1" >
Proof.<br/>
Let be $x,y : B$ and $p : x \equiv_{B} y$ and $q : x \equiv_{B} y$.
We need to prove $ p \equiv q$.<br/>
Since $A\simeq B$ then there is a function $f : A \to B$ and some
$g : B \to A$ such that $f \circ g \sim id_{B}$.
Using this function $g$ over the path $p$ we get
$$\mathsf{ap}_{g} p : g x \equiv_{A} g y$$.

We do the same but this time over the path $q$, that is,
$$\mathsf{ap}_{g} q : g x \equiv_{A} g y$$.
Because of $A$ is a set, we have a new path called
$$m :\mathsf{ap}_{g} p \equiv_{gx \equiv_{A} gy} \mathsf{ap}_{g} q$$. <br/>

Now, an action over this path $m$
using the function $$\mathsf{ap}_{f} : x \equiv_{A} y \to f x \equiv_{B} f y$$
will give us

$$
\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{ap}_{f}} m :
(\mathsf{ap}_{f}) (\mathsf{ap}_{g} p) \equiv (\mathsf{ap}_{f})  (\mathsf{ap}_{g} q).
$$


By the lemmas in Chapter 2, we do the following reasoning:

$$
\begin{align*}
(\mathsf{ap}_{f}) (\mathsf{ap}_{g} p) \equiv (\mathsf{ap}_{f})  (\mathsf{ap}_{g} q) &=
  \mathsf{ap}_{f \circ g} p \equiv \mathsf{ap}_{f \circ g} q\\
  &=(\text{transporting by using} f \sim g)\\
  &=\mathsf{ap}_{\id_{B}} p \equiv \mathsf{ap}_{\id_{B}} q\\
  &=p \equiv q.
\end{align*}
$$

Then, we have the inhabitant, $$\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{ap}_{f}} m : p \equiv q$$.
</div>

### Exercise 3.2

{: .exercise}
  Prove that if $A$ and $B$ are sets, then so is $A+B$.

To solve this exercise, we should take a look of some results from Chapter 2,
Section 2.12.

<div class="proof" id="proof-3.2" markdown="1">
Proof.<br/>

Let be $x, y : A + B$, and paths $p : x \equiv y$, $q : x \equiv
y$. Let's get a path $p \equiv q$.  We proceed by case analysis. If
$x :\equiv \mathsf{inl} a$ and $y :\equiv \mathsf{inl} b$, for
some $a, b : A$ then $$\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}^{-1}} p : a
\equiv_{A} b$$ and $$\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}^{-1}} q : a \equiv_{A}
b$$.

Since $A$ is a set, there is a path between these last two terms,
this is, $$m : \mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}^{-1}} p \equiv
\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}^{-1}} q$$.  Now, an action over this path
$$m$$ using the $$\mathsf{inl}$$ function give us:
$$\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}} m : \mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}}
(\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}^{-1}} p) \equiv \mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}}
(\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}^{-1}} q)$$.<br/>

By path algebra we have $$\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}}
m : p \equiv q$$ since $$\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}}
(\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}^{-1}} p) \equiv p$$.<br/> Following the
same reasoning, we prove the case $$x :\equiv \mathsf{inr} a$$ and $$y
:\equiv \mathsf{inr} b$$.  For the latest cases, $$x :\equiv
\mathsf{inl} a$$ and $$y :\equiv \mathsf{inr} b$$ and $$x :\equiv
\mathsf{inr} a$$ and $$y :\equiv \mathsf{inl} b$$, we use the
encode-decode method to derive a proof term for 𝟘 from
$p$ and $q$. Then, we may conclude anything we wish, that is, $p\equiv q$.
</div>

### Exercise 3.4

{: .exercise }
  Show that $A$ is a mere proposition if and only
  if $A\to A$ is contractible.

<div class="proof" markdown="1">
Proof. <br/>
- We must to show an inhabitant of the following type:

$$
\mathsf{isProp}(A) \to \sum\limits_{f : A \to A}\, \prod\limits_{g : A \to A } f = g.
$$

This is my proposed term:

$$
t :\equiv λ \mathsf{Aprop} \to (\id_{A}, λ (g : A \to A) \to \mathsf{funext} (\lambda (x : A) \to \mathsf{Aprop}~(\mathsf{id}~x)~(g~x)).
$$

- If $A → A$ is contractible, all functions in this type are equal,
then in particular given $x, y : A$, the constant functions $f(w) \equiv x$
and $g(w) \equiv y$ are equal. Then, $\mathsf{happly} (f =_{A \to A} g, w) : x = y$.
Therefore $$A$$ is a mere proposition.

</div>
